#### buttons to manipulate politics ###
#party_0 - attack and boost buttons are mutually exclusive

defined_text = {
	name = select_party1_ban_button

	#shows button in color
	text = {
		trigger = {
			if = { limit = { has_elections = no }
				has_political_power > 9
				else = { has_political_power > 99 }
			}
			#can't attack yourself or allies
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 0 }
					is_in_array = { gov_coalition_array = 0 }
				}
			}
		}
		localization_key = "GFX_ban_party_button"
	}
	#shows button, but in bw
	text = {
		localization_key = "GFX_ban_party_button_inactive"
	}
}

defined_text = {
	name = select_partyall_ban_button

	#shows button in color
	text = {
		trigger = {
			has_elections = no
			# can't if you already have em' banned
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = partyall_banned
			}
		}
		localization_key = "GFX_allow_party_button"
	}
	#shows button, but in bw
	text = {
		trigger = {
			has_elections = yes
			has_country_flag = partyall_banned
		}
		localization_key = "GFX_allow_party_button_inactive"
	}
}

defined_text = {
	name = select_party1_allow_button

	#shows button in color
	text = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = partyall_banned
			}
			has_political_power > 9
		}
		localization_key = "GFX_allow_party_button"
	}
	#shows button, but in bw
	text = {
		localization_key = "GFX_allow_party_button_inactive"
	}
}

			OR = {
				check_variable = { party_pop_elect_array^4 > election_threshold }
				check_variable = { party_pop_elect_array^5 > election_threshold }
				check_variable = { party_pop_elect_array^8 > election_threshold }
				check_variable = { party_pop_elect_array^9 > election_threshold }

				check_variable = { party_pop_elect_array^21 > election_threshold }
